<span id="freeTextContainer9564010015819404243">This is a good story. It kept me reading and left me curious for more when the last page turned. The writing, however, is basic and very much surface only. There were also a lot of small holes left with no understanding that really needed to be filled in order to actually grasp and connect with the characters and storyline. <br/><br/>I am interested to see if what I think will happen actually does, however. <br/>My predictions are that Elena is Blake’s Dragonrider (this is probably the biggest reason I want to</span>
  <span id="freeText9564010015819404243" style="display:none">This is a good story. It kept me reading and left me curious for more when the last page turned. The writing, however, is basic and very much surface only. There were also a lot of small holes left with no understanding that really needed to be filled in order to actually grasp and connect with the characters and storyline. <br /><br />I am interested to see if what I think will happen actually does, however. <br />My predictions are that Elena is Blake’s Dragonrider (this is probably the biggest reason I want to continue because that would be awesome!) She is also the King’s daughter but was somehow snuck into the “normal” world to keep her safe. <br /><br />SO...not sure whether I will continue or not. I am curious and would love to see where the storyline goes but I’m not sure if that curiosity is enough to actually overcome this first book’s shortcomings enough to pay full price for future books.</span>

<div id="review_1564289514" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1564289514" />
    <a title="Kirsty (Amethyst Bookwyrm)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7436809-kirsty-amethyst-bookwyrm"><img alt="Kirsty (Amethyst Bookwyrm)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364999103p2/7436809.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1564289514?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsty (Amethyst Bookwyrm)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsty (Amethyst Bookwyrm)" href="/user/show/7436809-kirsty-amethyst-bookwyrm">Kirsty (Amethyst Bookwyrm)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7436809-kirsty-amethyst-bookwyrm?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7436809-kirsty-amethyst-bookwyrm?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564289514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4450882210983571391">Elena has been on the run all of her life with her father, even though she has no idea why, that is until a dragon kills her father. She wakes up in a mystical land called Paegeia, and is soon enrolled in a new school where she meets lots of new people, including those who are able to change into dragons. Elena is struggling to learn everything she needs to be able to understand this new world she finds herself in, and with a long thought dead sorcerer back and Elena has to find a way to save he</span>
  <span id="freeText4450882210983571391" style="display:none">Elena has been on the run all of her life with her father, even though she has no idea why, that is until a dragon kills her father. She wakes up in a mystical land called Paegeia, and is soon enrolled in a new school where she meets lots of new people, including those who are able to change into dragons. Elena is struggling to learn everything she needs to be able to understand this new world she finds herself in, and with a long thought dead sorcerer back and Elena has to find a way to save her new home.<br /><br />Firebolt was an OK book which in some points I found entertaining but mostly I found it to be predictable, forgettable and the story didn’t pick up until near the end. It felt too teenage for me and had too much school drama and the relationships, both romantic and non-romantic developed way too quickly. <br /><br />I felt Elena was very immature for a 16 year old, for example blushing whenever anyone mentioned sex, and gets over the death of her father and arriving in this new world too quickly and I just generally was not a fan of her. However, I did like some of the secondary characters, like her two friends Becky and Sammy. On the other hand the boys irritated me as Lucian was too perfect and his relationship with Elena seems very superficial. Blake was mysterious and a jerk and I do not get why so many people like his character.<br /><br />I have heard that the following books go downhill and I am not sure I want to carry one with The Dragonian series. <br /><br />This and my other reviews can be found at <a href="http://amethystbookwyrm.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Amethyst Bookwyrm</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4450882210983571391" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17213428830455829288">4.5/5<br/>I really enjoyed this! The world of dragons in this was so rich and fascinating. My only problem was that I was super confused in the beginning, but slowly things seemed to make sense. I wish there was a guide for this series about all the different types of dragons. I thought the writing was amazing and the narrator only enhanced the experience for me. The mystery in this story is on so many different levels and I can wait to see how they will all play out. </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1400078690" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2287621281315613847"><a href='https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2015/10/brfirebolt.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444608688i/16523933._SX540_.jpg' alt='brfirebolt' width='400' height='165' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><strong> Finished reading: October 10th 2015</strong><br/><a href='https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/06/45.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434336878i/15206244.jpg' alt='Rating 4,5qqq' width='101' height='26' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><blockquote>
<br/>"If your mind and heart are in the same place, you can do whatever you want."<br/>
</blockquote><br/><strong>
  *** A copy of this book was kindly provided to me in exchange for an honest review. Thank you! ***
</strong><br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<a href='https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/09/myrambles11.jpg' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414545099i/11665748.jpg' alt='myrambles1reviewqqq' width='163' height='35' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Laura at<strong><a href='https://lalasbookreviews.wordpress.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'> LaLa's Blog</a></strong> contacted me last month with the question if I wanted to receive an e-copy of <strong>Firebolt</strong> in exchange for an honest review (with the permission of the author <strong>Adrienne Woods</strong>). As soon as I saw the blurb and read it was about dragons, I was sol</span></span>
  <span id="freeText2287621281315613847" style="display:none"><a href="https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2015/10/brfirebolt.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444608688i/16523933._SX540_.jpg" alt="brfirebolt" width="400" height="165" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><strong> Finished reading: October 10th 2015</strong><br><a href="https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/06/45.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434336878i/15206244.jpg" alt="Rating 4,5qqq" width="101" height="26" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><blockquote>
<br>"If your mind and heart are in the same place, you can do whatever you want."<br>
</blockquote><br><strong>
  *** A copy of this book was kindly provided to me in exchange for an honest review. Thank you! ***
</strong><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<a href="https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/09/myrambles11.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414545099i/11665748.jpg" alt="myrambles1reviewqqq" width="163" height="35" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Laura at<strong><a href="https://lalasbookreviews.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> LaLa's Blog</a></strong> contacted me last month with the question if I wanted to receive an e-copy of <strong>Firebolt</strong> in exchange for an honest review (with the permission of the author <strong>Adrienne Woods</strong>). As soon as I saw the blurb and read it was about dragons, I was sold. Fantasy stories with dragons are among my favorites and<strong> Firebolt</strong> turned out to be even better than I was originally hoping for. I loved the idea of dragons being some kind of 'shapeshifters' and both dragons and humans attending the same magic school. The worldbuilding is excellently done and with a fast pace and easy-to-read prose this first book in <strong>The Dragonian</strong> series is without doubt a quick and entertaining read. I do have to comment that some aspects of the story are a bit predictable and the novel ended with a big cliffhanger, but those were only minor setbacks in an otherwise solid story. I will definitely continue this series as I'm really curious what is going to happen with the main characters and their world. Recommended if you enjoy YA fantasy novels!<br><br><a href="https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/09/shortsummary11.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414545099i/11665749.jpg" alt="shortsummary1reviewqqq" width="210" height="35" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Elena Watkins doesn't really believe in fairy tales, but her whole world is about to change as her father tells her they have to leave their home yet again. She thinks her dad is only paranoid, but it turns out he had an excellent reason to be on the run... And that night she sees her own father turn into a dragon to fight off more of these mythical creatures. Her father was killed and Elena now finds herself in a whole new world she doesn't really understand; she has a hard time taking it all in. Dragons and magic actually exist, those dragons can take a human form and she will have to attend a new magical school as well... And to make things worse, an evil sorcerer might be trying to make his comeback. How will she deal with all this?<br><br><a href="https://melovebooks.files.wordpress.com/2014/08/finalthoughts.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414545099i/11665750.jpg" alt="finalthoughtsreviewqqq" width="210" height="35" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>I had some minor problems with<strong> Firebolt</strong> that prevented me from giving it the full five stars, but it is easy to say that I more than enjoyed this read. I love dragons in general and I really enjoyed picturing <strong>Adrienne Woods</strong>' version of them. The shapeshifter element is a nice twist and I liked the fact that the humans can learn to bond and ride with them. Some parts of the plot were quite predictable (I won't go into details to avoid spoilers), but the plot and worldbuilding were interesting enough for me to forget about it. If you like YA fantasy novels and enjoy dragon stories as much as I do, make sure to check out this series! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>P.S. Find more of my reviews <a href="http://melovebooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.</i>
</b>. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1916654145?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katarina" href="/user/show/1563554-katarina">Katarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780998471426" href="/book/show/33379357-firebolt">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1916654145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13997974198040574503">Now that I've read all five books and two Dragonian novellas, I feel like I can finally write a review for the series as a whole. <br/>I've read some of the reviews on Goodreads and noticed that people keep complaining about the writing style. English is not my first language, so I feel like I am not really competent to talk about that. That is why I will stick to the parts that I can give my opinion of- general plot, world building and character development.<br/>To some of you that have read my previous </span>
  <span id="freeText13997974198040574503" style="display:none">Now that I've read all five books and two Dragonian novellas, I feel like I can finally write a review for the series as a whole. <br />I've read some of the reviews on Goodreads and noticed that people keep complaining about the writing style. English is not my first language, so I feel like I am not really competent to talk about that. That is why I will stick to the parts that I can give my opinion of- general plot, world building and character development.<br />To some of you that have read my previous reviews may come as no surprise that I find character development to be almost most important part of any story. Characters are what keep the story going. <br />We had a plenty of development here, that I must say. <br />The world this story is set in was really interesting, as well as the magic system. I haven't read that many dragon books to say if it was unique enough, but I really enjoyed reading about it. <br />I found the plot to be a bit inconsistent. There were a lot unnecessary parts and I can't help the feeling that this could have been a much better trilogy than a five book series that it was. <br />Now... About the thing that most people found irritating. HP similarities. <br />Let me put it this way. If you start reading these books expecting them to be YA Harry Potter with a great accent on dragons, you will enjoy yourself, that's for sure. If not... You may be really annoyed. <br />There is a professor Trelawney in this book (with a different name, of course) and her eyes glow when she predicts something right. There is a lake that shows our heart's greatest desires (The Mirror of Erised). There is a village near school that students like visiting (Hogsmeade Village). And so on, and so on. <br />And, something else I just had to mention. <br />A lot of giggles.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13997974198040574503" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_734649647" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734649647" />
    <a title="Cassie C" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4479550-cassie-c"><img alt="Cassie C" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1482634975p2/4479550.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734649647?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cassie C" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cassie C" href="/user/show/4479550-cassie-c">Cassie C</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781491244654" href="/book/show/18305603-firebolt">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734649647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9451279584395213801">Actual rating: 4.5 stars<br/><br/>This was a fantastic start to a brand new series about dragons! This book originally caught my eye for two reasons. One, I love the cover, but two because it's about dragons!! There aren't many dragon themed books out there, so it allows the author to craft their own world. And Ms. Woods did an excellent job at this. I absolutely loved the unique and creatively built world that is Paegeia. There were breathtaking moments, and tons of heart-pounding action, perfect for any</span>
  <span id="freeText9451279584395213801" style="display:none">Actual rating: 4.5 stars<br /><br />This was a fantastic start to a brand new series about dragons! This book originally caught my eye for two reasons. One, I love the cover, but two because it's about dragons!! There aren't many dragon themed books out there, so it allows the author to craft their own world. And Ms. Woods did an excellent job at this. I absolutely loved the unique and creatively built world that is Paegeia. There were breathtaking moments, and tons of heart-pounding action, perfect for any reader who enjoys a good adventure book.<br /><br />The characters were great as well. Elena, who is literally introduced to the world of dragons by being thrown into the fire, was an awesome lead character. She reacted exactly how any person would, and was extremely relatable. Her character never seemed fake or annoying, and I greatly enjoyed that we learned more about the world as she did. It was an interesting journey from beginning to end. Elena's two best friends, Becky and Sammy, were also great side characters. However, they never fell into the background. They were constantly present throughout the story, and it was refreshing to read. Blake is certainly an interesting character, who is definitely a more-than-meets-the-eye type. I can't wait to find out more about him. Finally, Lucian. Ummm...can I just say how much I love him!!! 'Nuff said ;)<br /><br />The writing was great, however there were a couple of reasons I had to go down a star. First, there were some errors, and it did distract me a couple times when I had to figure out what was actually meant. Also, Elena used the phrase, "for the love of blueberries" a lot. The first couple of times, I thought it was funny, but it got old after a while. There were also a couple times I was confused about what dragon did what, so a glossary would have majorly helped, but other than that, this story was an amazing start to the series, and I can't wait until the next one comes out. This novel is chock full of action, romance, and humor. This is a must read for anyone! Happy reading :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9451279584395213801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Sb5Ha9hLPLrwE/xworvC97EwaFXKFz8qPoF+SpqqzbJlZczwkK4F19GnmNKDrjXZjfLx9BoWR8UE3vkr9NQZyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xFWms8rjlSvsfJi2Lxr+PKUjLLttKlNEYV2xodFRVmXoji0oggasRs3I/BQODwkSmeG1Gr0rK6tbAjbAvy+CHQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
